\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
\subsubsection*{template$<$typename \+\_\+\+Scalar, int \+\_\+\+Block\+At\+Compile\+Time, int \+\_\+\+Options, typename \+\_\+\+Storage\+Index$>$\newline
class Eigen\+::\+Block\+Sparse\+Matrix$<$ \+\_\+\+Scalar, \+\_\+\+Block\+At\+Compile\+Time, \+\_\+\+Options, \+\_\+\+Storage\+Index $>$}
A versatile sparse matrix representation where each element is a block. 

This class provides routines to manipulate block sparse matrices stored in a BSR-\/like representation. There are two main types \+:


\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item All blocks have the same number of rows and columns, called block size in the following. In this case, if this block size is known at compile time, it can be given as a template parameter like 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1BlockSparseMatrix_a80ff095a189183a0fb957cdf0906af89}{BlockSparseMatrix<Scalar,\ 3,\ ColMajor>}}\ bmat(b\_rows,\ b\_cols);}

\end{DoxyCode}
 Here, bmat is a b\+\_\+rows x b\+\_\+cols block sparse matrix where each coefficient is a 3x3 dense matrix. If the block size is fixed but will be given at runtime, 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1BlockSparseMatrix_a80ff095a189183a0fb957cdf0906af89}{BlockSparseMatrix<Scalar,\ Dynamic,\ ColMajor>}}\ bmat(b\_rows,\ b\_cols);}
\DoxyCodeLine{bmat.setBlockSize(block\_size);}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item The second case is for variable-\/block sparse matrices. Here each block has its own dimensions. The only restriction is that all the blocks in a row (resp. a column) should have the same number of rows (resp. of columns). It is thus required in this case to describe the layout of the matrix by calling set\+Block\+Layout(row\+Blocks, col\+Blocks).
\end{DoxyEnumerate}

In any of the previous case, the matrix can be filled by calling \doxylink{classEigen_1_1BlockSparseMatrix_aa148b63f89555f4eed312638abe597eb}{set\+From\+Triplets()}. A regular sparse matrix can be converted to a block sparse matrix and vice versa. It is obviously required to describe the block layout beforehand by calling either \doxylink{classEigen_1_1BlockSparseMatrix_a1984d81fa41dc2f4e8f1208f602e7e45}{set\+Block\+Size()} for fixed-\/size blocks or set\+Block\+Layout for variable-\/size blocks.


\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}
{\em \+\_\+\+Scalar} & The Scalar type \\
\hline
{\em \+\_\+\+Block\+At\+Compile\+Time} & The block layout option. It takes the following values Dynamic \+: block size known at runtime a numeric number \+: fixed-\/size block known at compile time \\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

Assignment from a sparse matrix with the same storage order. 

Convert from a sparse matrix to block sparse matrix. \begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
Before calling this function, tt is necessary to call either \doxylink{classEigen_1_1BlockSparseMatrix_acad69e4bb5e747db973cacc75c2f4a4d}{set\+Block\+Layout()} (matrices with variable-\/size blocks) or \doxylink{classEigen_1_1BlockSparseMatrix_a1984d81fa41dc2f4e8f1208f602e7e45}{set\+Block\+Size()} (for fixed-\/size blocks). 
\end{DoxyWarning}

template$<$typename \+\_\+\+Scalar , int \+\_\+\+Block\+At\+Compile\+Time, int \+\_\+\+Options, typename \+\_\+\+Storage\+Index $>$ \\
void \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1BlockSparseMatrix}{Eigen\+::\+Block\+Sparse\+Matrix}}$<$ \+\_\+\+Scalar, \+\_\+\+Block\+At\+Compile\+Time, \+\_\+\+Options, \+\_\+\+Storage\+Index $>$\+::reserve (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceEigen_a62e77e0933482dafde8fe197d9a2cfde}{Index}}}]{nonzerosblocks}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Allocate the internal array of pointers to blocks and their inner indices. 

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
For fixed-\/size blocks, call \doxylink{classEigen_1_1BlockSparseMatrix_a1984d81fa41dc2f4e8f1208f602e7e45}{set\+Block\+Size()} to set the block. And For variable-\/size blocks, call \doxylink{classEigen_1_1BlockSparseMatrix_acad69e4bb5e747db973cacc75c2f4a4d}{set\+Block\+Layout()} before using this function
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em nonzerosblocks} & Number of nonzero blocks. The total number of nonzeros is is computed in \doxylink{classEigen_1_1BlockSparseMatrix_acad69e4bb5e747db973cacc75c2f4a4d}{set\+Block\+Layout()} for variable-\/size blocks \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\end{DoxySeeAlso}

Allocate the internal array of pointers to blocks and their inner indices. 

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
For fixed-\/size blocks, call \doxylink{classEigen_1_1BlockSparseMatrix_a1984d81fa41dc2f4e8f1208f602e7e45}{set\+Block\+Size()} to set the block. And For variable-\/size blocks, call \doxylink{classEigen_1_1BlockSparseMatrix_acad69e4bb5e747db973cacc75c2f4a4d}{set\+Block\+Layout()} before using this function
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}

Set the row and column block layouts,. 

This function set the size of each row and column block. So this function should be used only for blocks with variable size. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}

\hline
{\em col\+Blocks} & \+: Number of columns per column block \\

Call this only for fixed-\/size blocks \Hypertarget{classEigen_1_1BlockSparseMatrix_a40891e477661e68bc870319d1379c7aa}\index{Eigen::BlockSparseMatrix$<$ \_Scalar, \_BlockAtCompileTime, \_Options, \_StorageIndex $>$@{Eigen::BlockSparseMatrix$<$ \_Scalar, \_BlockAtCompileTime, \_Options, \_StorageIndex $>$}!setBlockStructure@{setBlockStructure}}

void \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1BlockSparseMatrix}{Eigen\+::\+Block\+Sparse\+Matrix}}$<$ \+\_\+\+Scalar, \+\_\+\+Block\+At\+Compile\+Time, \+\_\+\+Options, \+\_\+\+Storage\+Index $>$\+::set\+Block\+Structure (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const Matrix\+Type \&}]{block\+Pattern}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Set the nonzero block pattern of the matrix. 

Given a sparse matrix describing the nonzero block pattern, this function prepares the internal pointers for values. After calling this function, any {\itshape nonzero} block (bi, bj) can be set with a simple call to coeff\+Ref(bi,bj).

\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
Before calling this function, tt is necessary to call either \doxylink{classEigen_1_1BlockSparseMatrix_acad69e4bb5e747db973cacc75c2f4a4d}{set\+Block\+Layout()} (matrices with variable-\/size blocks) or \doxylink{classEigen_1_1BlockSparseMatrix_a1984d81fa41dc2f4e8f1208f602e7e45}{set\+Block\+Size()} (for fixed-\/size blocks).
\end{DoxyWarning}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em block\+Pattern} & \doxylink{structEigen_1_1Sparse}{Sparse} matrix of boolean elements describing the block structure\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}

Set the nonzero block pattern of the matrix. 

Given a sparse matrix describing the nonzero block pattern, this function prepares the internal pointers for values. After calling this function, any {\itshape nonzero} block (bi, bj) can be set with a simple call to coeff\+Ref(bi,bj).

\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
Before calling this function, tt is necessary to call either \doxylink{classEigen_1_1BlockSparseMatrix_acad69e4bb5e747db973cacc75c2f4a4d}{set\+Block\+Layout()} (matrices with variable-\/size blocks) or \doxylink{classEigen_1_1BlockSparseMatrix_a1984d81fa41dc2f4e8f1208f602e7e45}{set\+Block\+Size()} (for fixed-\/size blocks).
\end{DoxyWarning}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classEigen_1_1BlockSparseMatrix_aa148b63f89555f4eed312638abe597eb} 
template$<$typename \+\_\+\+Scalar , int \+\_\+\+Block\+At\+Compile\+Time, int \+\_\+\+Options, typename \+\_\+\+Storage\+Index $>$ \\

void \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1BlockSparseMatrix}{Eigen\+::\+Block\+Sparse\+Matrix}}$<$ \+\_\+\+Scalar, \+\_\+\+Block\+At\+Compile\+Time, \+\_\+\+Options, \+\_\+\+Storage\+Index $>$\+::set\+From\+Triplets (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const Input\+Iterator \&}]{begin}{, }\item[{const Input\+Iterator \&}]{end}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Fill values in a matrix from a triplet list. 

Each triplet item has a block stored in an \doxylink{namespaceEigen}{Eigen} dense matrix. The Input\+Iterator class should provide the functions \doxylink{classEigen_1_1SparseMatrixBase_a4eb3c5bb9f26cf66f992e6d96d384f9a}{row()}, \doxylink{classEigen_1_1SparseMatrixBase_afecb59867e6df678c54c4c418365b076}{col()} and \doxylink{abseil-cpp_2absl_2container_2flat__hash__map__test_8cc_a54c2bae0f8aeed048a397b0618037252}{value()}

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
For fixed-\/size blocks, call \doxylink{classEigen_1_1BlockSparseMatrix_a1984d81fa41dc2f4e8f1208f602e7e45}{set\+Block\+Size()} before this function.
\end{DoxyNote}
